[30;1m1 | [0m[35m---[0m
[30;1m2 | [0m[35mfixes:[0m
[30;1m3 | [0m[35m  - |[0m
[30;1m4 | [0m[35m    Reap the rootwrap daemon process after it is timeout and quit. When the[0m

[30;1m6 | [0m[35m    it. Fixed this behaviour by adding a thread to wait the process to be done[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35m    once the daemon is started.[0m
